0                                  22350              *
                                   22351              *
                                   22352              *  GET UNIQUE NUMBER FOR DUPLICATE SESSION
                                   22353              *
                                   22354              *  RETURNS:
                                   22355              *        R15 - UNIQUE SESSION NUMBER FOR DUPLICATE LOGONS
                                   22356              *
                                   22357              *  BY DUPLICATE LOGON, WE MEAN MULTIPLE SESSIONS FOR A
                                   22358              *  SINGLE ACCOUNT
                                   22359              *
                                   22360              *  WE GET UNUSED SESSION NUMBER BY MARKING ALL USED SESSION
                                   22361              *  NUMBERS IN AN BYTE ARRAY THAT IS MAX NUMBER OF SESSIONS
                                   22362              *  LONG (PLUS A LITTLE BIT).  WE THEN FIND THE FIRST UNUSED
                                   22363              *  SESSION NUMBER BY LOOKING FOR THE FIRST ZERO IN THE ARRAY.
                                   22364              *
                                   22365              *  FOR PSEUDO SESSIONS:
                                   22366              *  THE SESSION NUMBER OF '9663' SHOULD SIMPLY BE HIGHER
                                   22367              *  THAN THE MAXIMUM NUMBER OF USERS WE WOULD EVER HAVE.
                                   22368              *  SPIRES FOR SOME REASON WANTS A NUMBER THAT MODULO 64
                                   22369              *  IS 63 ...  9663 WORKS, BUT THERE IS NOTHING SPECIAL
                                   22370              *  ABOUT THIS NUMBER.  THE ARRAY SCHEME MENTIONED ABOVE
                                   22371              *  IS USED TO FIND UNIQUE PSUEDO SESSION NUMBERS ...
                                   22372              *  ...  9663, 9662, 9661, 9660, ETC ..

0                                  26994              *
                                   26995              *
                                   26996              *  ELF LOGIN:  PROCESS ELF DIRECT LOGIN
                                   26997              *
                                   26998              *  THIS ROUTINE PROCESSES 'LOGIN: ... ' STRING
                                   26999              *  PASSED BY ELF.  FOR NOW WE ONLY LOOK AT THE
                                   27000              *  ACCOUNT AND COMMAND FIELDS.  ALL OTHER FIELDS
                                   27001              *  ARE IGNORED.  SPECIFICALLY, THE PASSWORD FIELD
                                   27002              *  IS IGNORED.  IF AN ACCOUNT REQUIRES A PASSWORD,
                                   27003              *  THE USER WILL BE PROMPTED, EVEN IF ONE WAS SUPPLIED.
                                   27004              *  THE COMMAND WILL BE PASSED AS THE FIRST COMMAND.
                                   27005              *  (HMMM).
                                   27006              *
                                   27007              *  ON ENTRY:
                                   27008              *  THE SCAN CONTROL BLOCK POINTS JUST PAST THE 'LOGIN: '
                                   27009              *
                                   27010              *  ON EXIT:
                                   27011              *  CPCACCT AND CPCMD,CPCMDLEN ARE SET APPROPRIATELY
                                   27012              *
                                   27013              *  ERRORS:
                                   27014              *  FOR NOW (EVER),  BAD SCANS SHOULD SET R15=4 (NZ) AND NOT
                                   27015              *  GIVE ANY ERROR MSGS.  UNRECOGNIZED OPTIONS FROM ELF SHOULD BE
                                   27016              *  IGNORED.
                                   27017              *
                                   27018              *  THIS ROUTINES IS CALLED BY 'SCAN SIGNPRT'.
                                   27019              *
